In reply to this message
Characteristics of Uniform Flow in Open channels:

For any channel of given roughness, cross section and slope, there exists one and only one water depth called the normal depth, at which the flow will be uniform.
Given steady flow conditions, the uniform flow will eventually be established in any channel which continues sufficiently far with constant slope and cross-section.
The bed slope, energy slope and water surface slope all are parallel to each other i.e. So = Sf = Sw.
Depth and velocity of flow are constant throughout the length of the channel.
The Head loss between in any two sections having length, ‚ÄòL‚Äô in case of uniform flow is given as:
HL = S0L;

Manning‚Äôs formula and Chezy‚Äôs formula can be used for uniform flow for evaluation of velocity of flow:
